          className="ml-2 bg-black text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm hover:bg-gray-800 transition"
          data-testid="add-income-btn"
          type="button"
          onClick={addIncome}
        >
          Add
        </button>
      </div>
    </form>
  );
};

const ExpenseForm = ({ onAddExpense }) => {

    setExpense("");

  return (
    <form className="flex-1 bg-white rounded-xl shadow p-5 flex flex-col items-start gap-6 min-w-[320px]">

          data-testid="add-expense-btn"
          type="button"
          onClick={addExpense}
        >
          Add
        </button>
      </div>
    </form>
  );

const Summary = ({ totalInc, totalExp }) => {
  let Inc = totalInc;
  let Exp = totalExp;
  return (
    <div data-testid="summary" className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-8">
      <div
        data-testid="total-income"
        className="flex-1 bg-white rounded-xl shadow p-6 min-w-[200px]"
      >
        <div className="text-gray-600 text-sm mb-2">Total Income</div>
        <div className="text-4xl font-bold text-[#18A149]">
          \{totalInc.toFixed(2)}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div
        data-testid="total-expenses"
        className="flex-1 bg-white rounded-xl shadow p-6 min-w-[200px]"
      >
        <div className="text-gray-600 text-sm mb-2">Total Expenses</div>
        <div className="text-4xl font-bold text-[#D92D20]">
          \{totalExp.toFixed(2)}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div
        data-testid="balance"
        className="flex-1 bg-white rounded-xl shadow p-6 min-w-[200px]"
      >
        <div className="text-gray-600 text-sm mb-2">Balance</div>
        <div className="text-4xl font-bold text-black">
          \{(Inc - Exp).toFixed(2)}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};








5. Color peaker
======================================
export default class ColorPicker extends Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { selectedColor: props.initialSelectedColor || "" };
  }

  handleSelect = (color) => {
    this.setState({ selectedColor: color });
  };

  render() {
    const { selectedColor } = this.state;
    const { colorPickerOptions } = this.props;
    return (
      <div>
        <div className="layout-row justify-content-center">
          <div className="card mt-75">
            <div
              style={{ background: selectedColor }}
              className="canvas"
              data-testid="selectedColor"
            >
              <p className="text-center mx-auto px-5">{selectedColor}</p>
            </div>
            <div className="card-actions">
              <div
                className="layout-row justify-content-center align-items-center"
                data-testid="colorPickerOptions"
              >
                {colorPickerOptions.map((color, index) => {
                  return (
                    <div
                      className={classNames({
                        "color-box": true,
                        "mx-8": true,
                        "my-15": true,
                        selected: selectedColor === color,
                      })}
                      key={color}
                      onClick={() => this.handleSelect(color)}
                      style={{ backgroundColor: color }}
                    ></div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
}

const App = () => {
  const [name, setName] = useState("");
  const [position, setPosition] = useState("");
  const [salary, setSalary] = useState("");
  const [list, setList] = useState(employeesList);

  return (
    <Fragment>
      <h8k-navbar header={title}></h8k-navbar>

        <table data-testid="table">

            <tr>
              <th>Name</th>
              <th>Position</th>
              <th>Salary</th>
              <th>Action</th>
            </tr>

                name={name}

                setList={setList}

        </table>
      </div>
    </Fragment>
  );
};



AddEmployee.js

const AddEmployee = ({
  name,
  setName,
  position,
  setPosition,
  salary,
  setSalary,
  list,
  setList,
}) => {
  const newEmp = { name: name, position: position, salary: salary };
  const addEmployee = () => {
    const arr = [...list, newEmp];
    setList(arr);
    setName("");
    setPosition("");
    setSalary("");
  };
  return (
    <Fragment>
      <td className="pl-30">
        <input
          value={name}
          onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
          data-testid="new-employee-name-input"
          placeholder="Enter Name"
        />
      </td>
      <td className="pl-20">
        <input
          value={position}
          onChange={(e) => setPosition(e.target.value)}
          data-testid="new-employee-position-input"
          placeholder="Enter Position"
        />
      </td>
      <td className="pl-20">
        <input
          value={salary}
          onChange={(e) => setSalary(e.target.value)}
          data-testid="new-employee-salary-input"
          type="number"
          placeholder="Enter Salary"
        />
      </td>
      <td className="pl-20">
        <button
          data-testid="add-new-employee-button"
          className="x-small w-75 ma-0 px-25"
          onClick={addEmployee}
          disabled={!name || !position || !salary}
        >
          Add
        </button>
      </td>
    </Fragment>
  );
};


Employee.js
-----------------------------------------
const Employee = ({ idx, employee }) => {
  const [emp, setEmp] = useState(employee);
  const [flag, setFlag] = useState(true);

  const salaryChange = (e) => {
    const value = e.target.value;
    setEmp((prev) => ({ ...prev, salary: value === "" ? "" : Number(value) }));
  };

  const divClick = () => {
    setFlag(false);
  };

  const handleSave = () => {
    setFlag(true);
  };
  return (
    <Fragment>
      <td>{employee.name}</td>
      <td className="pl-20">{employee.position}</td>
      <td className="pl-20">
        {flag ? (
          <div onClick={divClick} data-testid={"employee-salary-div-" + idx}>
            {emp.salary}
          </div>
        ) : (
          <input
            onChange={salaryChange}
            data-testid={"employee-salary-input-" + idx}
            type="number"
            value={emp.salary}
          />
        )}
      </td>
      <td className="pl-20">
        <button
          className={"x-small w-75 ma-0 px-25"}
          data-testid={"employee-save-button-" + idx}
          onClick={handleSave}
          disabled={emp.salary === employee.salary || flag}
        >
          Save
        </button>
      </td>
    </Fragment>
  );
};









7.Fetch-stock

function Users() {
  const [stock, setStock] = useState(stocks);
  const [month, setMonth] = useState("January");

  useEffect(() => {
    const filtered = stocks.filter((x) => x.date.includes("January"));
    setStock(filtered);
  }, []);

  const filterMonth = (e) => {
    let mon = e.target.value;
    setMonth(mon);
    const filtered = stocks.filter((x) => x.date.includes(mon));
    setStock(filtered);
  };

  const sorted = () => {
    const arr = [...stock].sort(
      (a, b) => b.close - b.open - (a.close - a.open)
    );
    setStock(arr);
  };

  let p = 0;
  let l = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < stock.length; i++) {
    if (stock[i].close - stock[i].open > 0) {
      p += stock[i].close - stock[i].open;
    } else {
      l += stock[i].close - stock[i].open;
    }
  }
  return (
    <>
      <div className="layout-row justify-content-center">
        <select
          value={month}
          className="mt-13 mr-5"
          onChange={filterMonth}
          data-testid="select-month"
        >
          <option>January</option>
          <option>February</option>
          <option>March</option>
          <option>April</option>
          <option>May</option>
          <option>June</option>
          <option>July</option>
          <option>August</option>
          <option>September</option>
          <option>October</option>
          <option>November</option>
          <option>December</option>
        </select>
        <button onClick={sorted} data-testid="sort">
          Sort
        </button>
      </div>
      <div
        className="layout-row wrap w-100 justify-content-center"
        data-testid="stocks"
      >
        {stock.map((item) => (
          <div className="card layout-column w-20 ma-10 px-8">
            <p className="ma-0">Date: {item.date}</p>
            <p className="ma-0">High: {item.high}</p>
            <p className="ma-0">Low: {item.low}</p>
            <p className="ma-0">
              Profit: {item.close - item.open > 0 ? "  " : "  "}(
              {Math.abs(item.close - item.open).toFixed(2)})
            </p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
      <div className="layout-column justify-content-center align-items-center">
        <p className="mb-0 font-weight-bold" data-testid="total-profit">
          Total Profit: <span style={{ color: "#1ba94c" }}>{p.toFixed(2)}</span>
        </p>
        <p className="font-weight-bold" data-testid="total-loss">
          Total Loss: <span style={{ color: "red" }}>{l.toFixed(2)}</span>
        </p>
      </div>
    </>
  );
}

const FlashCardDeck: React.FC<FlashCardDeckProps> = ({ flashCards }) => {
  const[cards, setCards]=useState(flashCards);
  const handleShuffle=()=>{
    const next =[...cards];
    [next[0], next[1]] =[next[1], next[0]]
    setCards(next)
  }
  return (
    <div className="layout-column align-items-center justify-content-start">
      <div className="flashcard-deck" data-testid="flashcard-deck">
        {cards.map((card, index)=>(

          <FlashCard key={index} flashCard={card} />
        ))}
      </div>
      <button onClick={handleShuffle} data-testid="shuffle-button">Shuffle</button>
    </div>
  );
};

9. Form validation
===============================================

function Form() {
  const [name, setName] = useState("");
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
  const [phone, setPhone] = useState("");
  const [url, setUrl] = useState("");
  const [submitted, setSubmitted] = useState(false);

  const validateName = (val) => {
    if (!val) return false;
    if (val.length > 25) return false;
    if (!/^[A-Za-z ]+\/.test(val)) return false;
    const lettercount = (val.match(/[A-Za-z]/g) || []).length;
    return lettercount >= 3;
  };

  const validatePhone = (val) => {
    if (!val) return false;
    return /^\d{10}\/.test(val);
  };


function validateEmail(email) {
  const regex = /^[a-zA-Z]{1}[a-zA-Z0-9]{2,19}@[a-zA-Z]{3,10}\.[a-zA-Z]{3,5}\/;
  return regex.test(email);
}

function validateUrl(url) {
  const regex = /https:\/\/[a-zA-Z]{3,10}.[a-zA-Z]{3,20}.[a-zA-Z]{2,5}\/;
  return regex.test(url);
}

  const isNameValid = validateName(name);
  const isEmailValid = validateEmail(email);
  const isPhoneValid = validatePhone(phone);
  const isUrlValid = validateUrl(url);

  const allValid = isNameValid && isEmailValid && isPhoneValid && isUrlValid;

  const onVerify = () => {
    setSubmitted(true);
  };
  return (
    <div className="card w-40 mx-auto py-50 px-50 my-10">
      <div>
        <div className="layout-column">
          <label htmlFor="name">Name</label>
          <input
            id="name"
            data-testid="name"
            placeholder="John Doe"
            className="large mt-8 px-10"
            value={name}
            onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
          />
          {submitted && !isNameValid && (
            <p
              data-testid="nameErrorTxt"
              className="form-hint error-text mx-10"
              id="hint-input"
            >
              Error: Invalid Entry
            </p>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div className="mt-15 layout-column">
          <label htmlFor="email">Email</label>
          <input
            id="email"
            data-testid="email"
            placeholder="johndoe@hackerrank.com"
            className="large mt-8 px-10"
            value={email}
            onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
          />
          {submitted && !isEmailValid && (
            <p
              data-testid="emailErrorTxt"
              className="form-hint error-text mx-10"
              id="hint-input"
            >
              Error: Invalid Entry
            </p>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div className="mt-15 layout-column">
          <label htmlFor="phone">Phone</label>
          <input
            id="phone"
            data-testid="phone"
            placeholder="1234567890"
            className="large mt-8 px-10"
            value={phone}
            onChange={(e) => setPhone(e.target.value)}
          />
          {submitted && !isPhoneValid && (
            <p
              data-testid="phoneErrorTxt"
              className="form-hint error-text mx-10"
              id="hint-input"
            >
              Error: Invalid Entry
            </p>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div className="mt-15 layout-column">
          <label htmlFor="blogUrl">Blog URL</label>
          <input
            id="blogUrl"
            data-testid="url"
            placeholder="https://www.johndoe.dev"
            className="large mt-8 px-10"
            value={url}
            onChange={(e) => setUrl(e.target.value)}
          />
          {submitted && !isUrlValid && (
            <p
              data-testid="urlErrorTxt"
              className="form-hint error-text mx-10"
              id="hint-input"
            >
              Error: Invalid Entry
            </p>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      <button
        onClick={onVerify}
        data-testid="verify"
        className="button mt-40"
        type="button"
      >
        VERIFY
      </button>
      {submitted && allValid && (
        <div
          data-testid="successMsg"
          className="success-text success-text text-center py-40"
        >
          Verification Successful
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}









10. Hacker-bank
----------------------------------------------------

function TransactionTable({ txns }) {
  const [data, setData] = useState(txns);
  const [input, setInput] = useState("2019-11-29");

  const sort = () => {
    const sorted = [...data].sort((x, y) => x.amount - y.amount);
    setData(sorted);
  };

  const findByDate = () => {
    const dateInput = document.getElementById("date").value;
    if (!input) return;
    const filtered = [...txns].filter((x) => x.date === input);
    setData(filtered);
  };
  return (
    <div className="layout-column align-items-center mt-50">
      <section className="layout-row align-items-center justify-content-center">
        <label className="mr-10">Transaction Date</label>
        <input
          id="date"
          type="date"
          defaultValue="2019-11-29"
          onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
          role="search"
        />
        <button onClick={findByDate} className="small">
          Filter
        </button>
      </section>

      <div className="card mt-50">
        <table className="table">
          <thead>
            <tr className="table">
              <th className="table-header">Date</th>
              <th className="table-header">Description</th>
              <th className="table-header">Type</th>
              <th className="table-header">
                <span id="amount" onClick={sort} role="button">
                  Amount (\)
                </span>
              </th>
              <th className="table-header">Available Balance</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody>
            {data.map((item, index) => (
              <tr key={index}>
                <td>{item.date}</td>
                <td>{item.description}</td>
                <td>{item.type === 1 ? "Debit" : "Credit"}</td>
                <td>{item.amount}</td>
                <td>{item.balance}</td>
              </tr>
            ))}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}









11.Hacker maps
===============================================

export default class Navigation extends Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = {
      locations: props.locations,
    };
  }

  // Used for rendering
  getClasses(ctx, index) {
    let classes = ^material-icons \{ctx}^;
    if (ctx === "dots") {
      if (this.isLast(index)) {
        classes += " hidden";
      }
    } else {
      classes += this.isLast(index) ? " small" : " x-small";
      if (index === 0) {
        classes += " first";
      }
    }
    return classes;
  }

  // Used for rendering
  isLast(index) {
    return index === this.props.locations.length - 1;
  }

  moveUp = (index) => {
    const data = [...this.state.locations];
    const temp = data[index];
    data[index] = data[index - 1];
    data[index - 1] = temp;
    this.setState({ locations: data });
  };

  moveDown = (index) => {
    const data = [...this.state.locations];
    const temp = data[index];
    data[index] = data[index + 1];
    data[index + 1] = temp;
    this.setState({ locations: data });
  };

  render() {
    const { locations } = this.state;
    return (
      <div className="layout-row align-items-center justify-content-center navigation-screen">
        <div className="card layout-row flat map-card">
          <section className="card pb-16 pr-16 flex-auto layout-column justify-content-center">
            <ul className="pl-0" data-testid="location-list">
              {/*Use this li for rendering each location item as it contains all the data-testid attributes required for the tests to pass*/}
              {locations.map((location, index) => (
                <li
                  key={"row" + index}
                  data-testid={"location-" + index}
                  className="layout-row justify-content-between align-items-center mr-8 pl-40 relative"
                >
                  <div className="layout-column justify-content-start align-items-center handle">
                    <i className={this.getClasses("marker", index)}>
                      {this.isLast(index) ? "room" : "radio_button_checked"}
                    </i>
                    <i className={this.getClasses("dots", index)}>more_vert</i>
                  </div>
                  <div className="location-name">
                    <p
                      className="caption text-start mb-4"
                      data-testid="location"
                    >
                      {location}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    {!(index === 0) && (
                      <button
                        className="icon-only small mx-0"
                        data-testid="up-button"
                        onClick={() => this.moveUp(index)}
                      >
                        <i className="material-icons">arrow_upward</i>
                      </button>
                    )}
                    {!(index === locations.length - 1) && (
                      <button
                        className="icon-only small mx-0"
                        data-testid="down-button"
                        onClick={() => this.moveDown(index)}
                      >
                        <i className="material-icons">arrow_downward</i>
                      </button>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </li>
              ))}
            </ul>
          </section>
          <section className="flex-auto">
            <img src="images/map.svg" className="fill" alt="map" />
          </section>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
}





12. Image-preview
====================================================

const ImagePreview = ({ images }) => {
  const [items, setItems] = useState(images);

  const imgToggle = (index) => {
    setItems((prev) =>
      prev.map((img, i) =>
        i === index ? { ...img, visible: !img.visible } : img
      )
    );
  };
  const handleShow = () => {
    setItems((prev) => prev.map((x) => ({ ...x, visible: true })));
  };

  const handleHide = () => {
    setItems((prev) => prev.map((x) => ({ ...x, visible: false })));
  };
  return (
    <div className="layout align-items-center mt-100">
      <div className="card ma-20 pa-50">
        <section>
          <div
            className="layout-row justify-content-around"
            data-testid="images-div"
          >
            {items.map((img, index) =>
              img.visible ? (
                <img
                  key={img.id}
                  src={img.src}
                  height={200}
                  width={300}
                  alt={img.all}
                  onClick={() => imgToggle(index)}
                />
              ) : (
                <HiddenImageDiv key={img.id} onClick={() => imgToggle(index)} />
              )
            )}
          </div>
        </section>
        <section className="card-actions justify-content-center">
          <button onClick={handleShow} data-testid="show-all-btn">
            Show all
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={handleHide}
            className="danger"
            data-testid="hide-all-btn"
          >
            Hide all
          </button>
        </section>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};












13. Instrusction board
===================================================

export default function InstructionBoard() {
  let [instructions, setInstructions] = React.useState([]);
  let [instruction, setInstruction] = React.useState("");
  const [errMsg, setErrMsg] = React.useState("");

  const addInstruction = (event) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    if (!instruction) {
      setErrMsg("Please enter an instruction.");
      return;
    }
    setInstructions([...instructions, instruction]);
    setInstruction("");
  };

  const swapDown = (index) => {
    let temp = instructions;
    let temp2 = temp[index];
    temp[index] = temp[index + 1];
    temp[index + 1] = temp2;
    setInstruction([]);
    setInstructions(temp);
  };

  const swapUp = (index) => {
    let temp = instructions;
    let temp2 = temp[index];
    temp[index] = temp[index - 1];
    temp[index - 1] = temp2;
    setInstruction([]);
    setInstructions(temp);
  };

  return (
    <div className="mt-50 layout-column justify-content-center align-items-center">
      <div>
        <form onSubmit={addInstruction}>
          <section
            className="my-30 layout-row align-items-center justify-content-center"
            style={{ width: "1000px" }}
          >
            <input
              id="instruction-input"
              type="text"
              placeholder="New Instruction"
              data-testid="instruction-input"
              style={{ width: "80%" }}
              value={instruction}
              onChange={(e) => setInstruction(e.target.value)}
            />
            <button
              type="submit"
              className="ml-30"
              data-testid="add-instruction-button"
              style={{ width: "20%" }}
            >
              Add Instruction
            </button>
          </section>
        </form>
        {errMsg !== "" && (
          <span data-testid="error-message" className="error">
            {errMsg}
          </span>
        )}
      </div>
      <div className="card outlined mt-0" style={{ width: "800px" }}>
        <div className="card-text">
          <h4>Instructions</h4>
          <ul className="styled mt-50" data-testid="instructions">
            {instructions.map((instruction, i) => (
              <li
                className="slide-up-fade-in"
                key={i}
                data-testid={^instruction-\{instruction
                  .split(" ")
                  .join("-")}-li^}
              >
                <div className="li-content layout-row justify-content-between align-items-center py-10">
                  <span data-testid={^\{i + 1}^}>{i + 1}</span>
                  <span
                    data-testid={^instruction-\{instruction
                      .split(" ")
                      .join("-")}^}
                  >
                    {instruction}
                  </span>
                  <div className="icons">
                    <button
                      disabled={i === instructions.length - 1}
                      className="icon-only x-medium mx-2"
                      data-testid={^\{i}-swap-down^}
                      onClick={() => swapDown(i)}
                    >
                      <i className="material-icons">arrow_drop_down_icon</i>
                    </button>
                    <button
                      disabled={i === 0}
                      className="icon-only x-medium mx-2"
                      data-testid={^\{i}-swap-up^}
                      onClick={() => swapUp(i)}
                    >
                      <i className="material-icons">arrow_drop_up_icon</i>
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </li>
            ))}
          </ul>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}







14. Job application
======================================================

job application.jsx
---------------------------------
const JobApplicationForm = () => {
  const [name, setName] = useState("");
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
  const [experience, setExperience] = useState("");
  const [error, setError] = useState(false);
  const [flag, setFlag] = useState(false);
  const [data, setData] = useState("");

  const handleReset = () => {
    setName("");
    setEmail("");
    setExperience("");
  };

  const handlePreview = () => {
    if (!name.trim() || !email.trim || !Number(experience) < 0) {
      setError(true);
      return;
    }

    setData({ name, email, experience });
    setFlag(true);
    setName("");
    setEmail("");
    setExperience("");
  };
  return flag ? (
    <Preview onReset={handleReset} d={data} />
  ) : (
    <form data-testid="job-application-form" className="layout-column ml-auto">
      <h2 className="ma-auto pa-20">Provide your details</h2>
      <div>
        <label className="font-weight-bold">
          Name:
          <input
            data-testid="input-name"
            type="text"
            name="name"
            value={name}
            className="pa-10 ml-120"
            onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
          />
        </label>
        {error && (
          <p data-testid="error-name" className="error">
            Name is required.
          </p>
        )}
      </div>
      <div>
        <label className="font-weight-bold">
          Email:
          <input
            data-testid="input-email"
            type="email"
            name="email"
            value={email}
            className="pa-10 ml-120"
            onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
          />
        </label>
        {error && (
          <p data-testid="error-email" className="error">
            Enter a valid email address.
          </p>
        )}
      </div>
      <div>
        <label className="font-weight-bold">
          Experience (years):
          <input
            data-testid="input-experience"
            type="text"
            name="experience"
            value={experience}
            className="pa-10 ml-20"
            onChange={(e) => setExperience(e.target.value)}
          />
        </label>
        {error && (
          <p data-testid="error-experience" className="error">
            Experience must be a positive number.
          </p>
        )}
      </div>
      <div className="ml-100">
        <button
          onClick={handlePreview}
          data-testid="preview-button"
          type="submit"
          className="mx-50"
        >
          Preview
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={handleReset}
          data-testid="reset-button"
          type="button"
          className="mx-50"
        >
          Reset
        </button>
      </div>
    </form>
  );
};




Preview.js
----------------------------------------------
const Preview = ({ onReset, d }) => {
  const [flag, setFlag] = useState(false);
  const [flags, setFlags] = useState(false);

  const handleClear = () => {
    setFlag(true);
    onReset();
  };

  const handleSubmit = () => {
    setFlags(true);
  };
  return flag ? (
    <JobApplicationForm />
  ) : flags ? (
    <SuccessMessage />
  ) : (
    <div data-testid="preview">
      <h2>Preview Your Application</h2>
      <p data-testid="preview-name">
        <strong>Name:</strong> {d.name}
      </p>
      <p data-testid="preview-email">
        <strong>Email:</strong> {d.email}
      </p>
      <p data-testid="preview-experience">
        <strong>Experience:</strong> {d.experience} years
      </p>
      <button onClick={handleClear} data-testid="clear-button">
        Clear
      </button>
      <button onClick={handleSubmit} data-testid="submit-button">
        Submit
      </button>
    </div>
  );
};



SuccessMessage.js
---------------------------------------------
const SuccessMessage = () => {
  const [flag, setFlag] = useState(false);
  const handleHome = () => {
    setFlag(true);
  };
  return flag ? (
    <JobApplicationForm />
  ) : (
    <div data-testid="success-message">
      <h2>Application Submitted Successfully!</h2>
      <p>Thank you for your application. We will review it soon.</p>
      <button
        onClick={handleHome}
        className="ma-auto"
        data-testid="reset-button"
      >
        Home
      </button>
    </div>
  );
};







15. Kanban board
======================================================
export default function KanbanBoard(props) {
  let [tasks, setTasks] = React.useState([
    { name: "1", stage: 0 },
    { name: "2", stage: 0 },
  ]);

  let [stagesNames, setStagesNames] = React.useState([
    "Backlog",
    "To Do",
    "Ongoing",
    "Done",
  ]);

  const [input, setInput] = useState("");

  const addTask = () => {
    if (!input) return;
    const newTask = { name: input, stage: 0 };
    setTasks([...tasks, newTask]);
    setInput("");
  };

  const deleteTask = (name) => {
    const filtered = [...tasks].filter((x) => x.name !== name);
    setTasks(filtered);
  };

  const moveTask = (name, dir) => {
    let newStage = [...tasks]?.find((x) => x.name === name).stage + dir;
    if (newStage < 0) newStage = 0;
    else if (newStage === stagesNames.length - 1)
      newStage = stagesNames.length - 1;

    const newTask = { name: name, stage: newStage };
    const filtered = [...tasks].filter((x) => x.name !== name);
    setTasks([...filtered, newTask]);
  };

  let stagesTasks = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < stagesNames.length; ++i) {
    stagesTasks.push([]);
  }
  for (let task of tasks) {
    const stageId = task.stage;
    stagesTasks[stageId].push(task);
  }

  return (
    <div className="mt-20 layout-column justify-content-center align-items-center">
      <section className="mt-50 layout-row align-items-center justify-content-center">
        <input
          id="create-task-input"
          type="text"
          className="large"
          placeholder="New task name"
          data-testid="create-task-input"
          value={input}
          onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
        />
        <button
          type="submit"
          className="ml-30"
          data-testid="create-task-button"
          onClick={addTask}
        >
          Create task
        </button>
      </section>

      <div className="mt-50 layout-row">
        {stagesTasks.map((tasks, i) => {
          return (
            <div className="card outlined ml-20 mt-0" key={^\{i}^}>
              <div className="card-text">
                <h4>{stagesNames[i]}</h4>
                <ul className="styled mt-50" data-testid={^stage-\{i}^}>
                  {tasks.map((task, index) => {
                    return (
                      <li className="slide-up-fade-in" key={^\{i}\{index}^}>
                        <div className="li-content layout-row justify-content-between align-items-center">
                          <span
                            data-testid={^\{task.name
                              .split(" ")
                              .join("-")}-name^}
                          >
                            {task.name}
                          </span>
                          <div className="icons">
                            <button
                              className="icon-only x-small mx-2"
                              data-testid={^\{task.name
                                .split(" ")
                                .join("-")}-back^}
                              disabled={task.stage === 0}
                              onClick={() => moveTask(task.name, -1)}
                            >
                              <i className="material-icons">arrow_back</i>
                            </button>
                            <button
                              className="icon-only x-small mx-2"
                              data-testid={^\{task.name
                                .split(" ")
                                .join("-")}-forward^}
                              disabled={task.stage === stagesNames.length - 1}
                              onClick={() => moveTask(task.name, 1)}
                            >
                              <i className="material-icons">arrow_forward</i>
                            </button>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => deleteTask(task.name)}
                              className="icon-only danger x-small mx-2"
                              data-testid={^\{task.name
                                .split(" ")
                                .join("-")}-delete^}
                            >
                              <i className="material-icons">delete</i>
                            </button>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </li>
                    );
                  })}
                </ul>
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}








16. Movie booking
======================================================
export const TicketBooking = () => {
  const rows = 10;
  const cols = 10;
  const [boookedSeats, setBookedSeats] = React.useState([]);
  const [selectedSeats, setSelectedSeats] = React.useState([]);

  const booking = () => {
    if (selectedSeats.length === 0) {
      alert("Please select at least one seat");
      return;
    }

    setBookedSeats([...boookedSeats, ...selectedSeats]);
    setSelectedSeats([]);
  };
  const clearing = () => {
    setSelectedSeats([]);
  };

  const resetting = () => {
    setBookedSeats([]);
    setSelectedSeats([]);
  };

  const seatToggle = (id) => {
    setSelectedSeats((prev) =>
      prev.includes(id) ? prev.filter((x) => x !== id) : [...prev, id]
    );
  };

  const seatClass = (id) =>
    boookedSeats.includes(id)
      ? "disabled seat"
      : selectedSeats.includes(id)
      ? "selected seat"
      : "seat";

  let seatRowsTimeAuto = "";
  for (let i = 0; i <= cols; i++) {
    seatRowsTimeAuto += "auto ";
  }
  return (
    <div className="mt-50 layout-column justify-content-center align-items-center">
      <div className="display-flex">
        <button onClick={booking} data-testid="book-seats">
          Book Seats
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={clearing}
          data-testid="clear-selection"
          className="danger"
        >
          Clear
        </button>
      </div>
      <div
        style={{ display: "grid", gridTemplateColumns: ^\{seatRowsTimeAuto}^ }}
      >
        {Array(rows)
          .fill(0)
          .map((_, row) => (
            <div key={row} style={row === 4 ? { marginRight: "40px" } : null}>
              {Array(cols)
                .fill(0)
                .map((_, col) => (
                  <div
                    onClick={() => seatToggle(^\{row}\{col}^)}
                    data-testid={^\{row}\{col}^}
                    className={seatClass(^\{row}\{col}^)}
                    key={^\{row}\{col}^}
                  >{^\{String.fromCharCode(65 + col)}\{row}^}</div>
                ))}
            </div>
          ))}
      </div>
      <br />
      <button onClick={resetting} data-testid="reset">
        Reset Bookings
      </button>
    </div>
  );
};





17. Movie-list
========================================================

function MovieList() {
  const [input, setInput] = useState();
  const [movies, setMovies] = useState([]);
  const [searched, setSearched] = useState(false);

  const search = async () => {
    const year = Number(input.trim());
    if (!year) return;
    try {
      const data = await fetch(
        ^https://jsonmock.hackerrank.com/api/moviesdata?Year=\{year}^
      );
      const json = await data.json();

      const arr = Array.isArray(json?.data) ? json.data : [];
      setMovies(arr);
    } catch {
      setMovies([]);
    } finally {
      setSearched(true);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="layout-column align-items-center mt-50">
      <section className="layout-row align-items-center justify-content-center">
        <input
          type="number"
          className="large"
          placeholder="Enter Year eg 2015"
          data-testid="app-input"
          value={input}
          onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
        />
        <button onClick={search} className="" data-testid="submit-button">
          Search
        </button>
      </section>

      <ul className="mt-50 styled" data-testid="movieList">
        {movies.map((movie) => (
          <li key={movie.imdbId} className="slide-up-fade-in py-10">
            {movie.Title}
          </li>
        ))}
      </ul>
      {searched && movies.length === 0 && (
        <div className="mt-50 slide-up-fade-in" data-testid="no-result">
          No Results Found!
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

WatchlistApp
---------------------------------------------------
const movies = [
  { id: 1, title: "Inception" },
  { id: 2, title: "Interstellar" },
  { id: 3, title: "The Dark Knight" },
  { id: 4, title: "Dunkirk" },
  { id: 5, title: "The Shawshank Redemption" },
];
 
const WatchlistApp = () => {
  const [data, setData] = useState([]);
  const flag = false

  const isAvailable = (d) => {
    for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i].id === d.id && data[i].title === d.title) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  };

  const handleRemove = (d) => {
    const arr = [...data].filter((a) => a.title !== d.title && a.id !== d.id);
    setData(arr);
  };

  const handleClear = () => {
    setData([]);
  };

  const handleAdd = (m) => {
    
    setData([...data, m]);
  };


  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Movies</h2>
      <div className="movies-container">
        {movies.map((e) => {
          return <MovieCard movie={e} flag={flag} handleAdd={handleAdd} isAvailable={isAvailable} />
        })}
      </div>

      <Watchlist
        list={data}
        handleRemove={handleRemove}
        handleClear={handleClear}
      />
    </div>
  );
}; 



Watchlist
-----------------------------------------------------

const Watchlist = ({list, handleRemove, handleClear}) => {
  
  return (
    <div data-testid="watchlist-container">
      {/* Provide the total count of movies watchlisted */}
      <h2>Watchlist {<span>({list.length})</span>}</h2>
      {list.length === 0 ? (
        <p data-testid="watchlist-empty">Your watchlist is empty.</p>
      ) : (
        <div>
          <div data-testid="movie-container" className="movies-container">
            {list.map((e) => {
              return (
                <MovieCard movie={e} flag={true} handleRemove={handleRemove} />
              );
            })}
          </div>
          <button data-testid="clear-watchlist-btn" onClick={handleClear}>
            Clear Watchlist
          </button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};



Moviecard
--------------------------------------------------
const MovieCard = ({ movie, flag, handleAdd, handleRemove, isAvailable }) => {

  return (
    // set all data-testids according to the movie id.
    // Ex: on the movie card the data-testid for movie with id:1  will be movie-card-1
    <div className="movie-card" data-testid={^movie-card-\{movie.id}^}>
      <h3 data-testid={^movie-title-0^}>{movie.title}</h3>
      {flag ? (
        <button className="danger" data-testid={^remove-btn-\{movie.id}^}  onClick={()=>handleRemove(movie)}>
          Remove
        </button> 
      ) : (
        <button data-testid={^add-btn-\{movie.id}^} disabled={isAvailable(movie)} onClick={()=>handleAdd(movie)}>
          {/* "Added" */}
          Add to Watchlist
        </button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

20. currency converter

function CurrencyConvertor() {
  const [input, setInput] = useState(defaultInput);
  const [option, setOption] = useState(defaultCurrency);

  const rate = exchangeRates.find((x) => x.currency === option)?.rate || 1;
  const usdValue = (input * rate).toFixed(3);
  const clearing = () => {
    setInput(defaultInput);
    setOption(defaultCurrency);
  };
  return (
    <div>
      <div className="layout-row justify-content-space-evenly min-height mt-75">
        <div className="layout-column w-35 pa-30 card">
          <select
            onChange={(e) => setOption(e.target.value)}
            className="mb-10"
            data-testid="select-currency"
          >
            {exchangeRates.map((item) => (
              <option>{item.currency}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
          <input
            className="h-50"
            type="number"
            value={input}
            onKeyDown={preventNegative}
            placeholder={^Enter value in \{option}^}
            data-testid="input-value"
            onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
          />
        </div>

        <div className="layout-column w-35 pa-30 card">
          <h3 className="mb-10 mt-0">USD</h3>
          <input
            className="h-50"
            type="number"
            value={usdValue}
            readOnly
            data-testid="converted-value"
          />
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="layout-row justify-content-center pa-20">
        <button onClick={clearing} data-testid="clear-values">
          Clear Input
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

SearchCustoemr.js
-------------------------------------------------
function SearchCustomer() {
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const [data, setData] = useState(customers);

  const setCustomer = (text) => {
    setInput(text);

    if (!text) {
      setData(customers);
      return;
    }

    setData(
      customers.filter(
        (e) =>
          e.name.startsWith(text) ||
          e.location.startsWith(text) ||
          e.gender.startsWith(text)
      )
    );
  };
  return (
    <>
      <div className="layout-row align-items-center justify-content-center mt-30">
        <input
          className="large mx-20 w-20"
          data-testid="search-input"
          type="text"
          value={input}
          placeholder="Enter search term (Eg: Phil)"
          onChange={(e) => setCustomer(e.target.value)}
        />
      </div>
      <CustomerList customers={data} />
    </>
  );
}







23. Fitness
==========================================================


fitness tracker.js
-----------------------------------------------
  const [logs, setLogs] = useState([]);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  const validateAndAdd = ({ exe, dur, cal }) => {
    const exercise = (exe || "").trim();
    const duration = Number(dur.trim());
    const calorie = Number(cal.trim());

    if (!exercise) {
      setError("Exercise type must not be empty.");
      return false;
    }
    if (duration <= 0) {
      setError("Duration must be a positive number.");
      return false;
    }
    if (calorie <= 0) {
      setError("Calories must be a positive number.");
      return false;
    }

    const newData = {
      id: Date.now(),
      exe: exercise,
      dur: duration,
      cal: calorie,
    };

    setLogs((prev) => [...prev, newData]);
    setError("");
    return true;
  };

  const resetLogs = () => {
    setLogs([]);
    setError("");
  };

  return (
    <div className="pa-20">
      <h1>Track Your Fitness</h1>
      <LogForm reset={resetLogs} error={error} onValid={validateAndAdd} />
      <LogList logs={logs} />
    </div>
  );
};



logform.js
-----------------------------------------------------
const LogForm = ({ reset, onValid, error }) => {
  const [exe, setExe] = useState("");
  const [dur, setDur] = useState("");
  const [cal, setCal] = useState("");

  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    const valid = onValid({ exe, dur, cal });
    if (valid) {
      setExe("");
      setDur("");
      setCal("");
    }
  };

  const handleReset = () => {
    setExe("");
    setDur("");
    setCal("");
    reset();
  };

  return (
    <div className="layout column justify-content-center align-items-center">
      <form data-testid="log-form">
        <div className="mb-10">
          <label>
            Exercise Type:
            <input
              type="text"
              name="exerciseType"
              value={exe}
              placeholder="e.g., Running"
              className="ml-50"
              data-testid="input-exerciseType"
              required
              onChange={(e) => setExe(e.target.value)}
            />
          </label>
        </div>
        <div className="mb-10">
          <label>
            Duration (minutes):
            <input
              type="number"
              name="duration"
              value={dur}
              placeholder="e.g., 30"
              className="ml-10"
              data-testid="input-duration"
              required
              onChange={(e) => setDur(e.target.value)}
            />
          </label>
        </div>
        <div className="mb-10">
          <label>
            Calories Burned:
            <input
              type="number"
              name="caloriesBurned"
              value={cal}
              placeholder="e.g., 300"
              className="ml-30"
              data-testid="input-caloriesBurned"
              required
              onChange={(e) => setCal(e.target.value)}
            />
          </label>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={handleSubmit}
          type="submit"
          data-testid="btn-logActivity"
          className="mr-10"
        >
          Log Activity
        </button>
        <button onClick={handleReset} type="button" data-testid="btn-resetLog">
          Reset Log
        </button>
      </form>
      {error && (
        <p data-testid="error-message" style={{ color: "red" }}>
          {error}
        </p>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

24. Profile
====================================================

const Profile = () => {
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState({
    firstName: "Sherlock",
    lastName: "Holmes",
    email: "sherlockholmes@email.com",
  });
  const [data, setData] = useState(profile);
  const [isEditing, setIsEditing] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    if (!isEditing) {
      setData(profile);
      setIsEditing(true);
      return;
    }
    const { firstName, lastName, email } = data;

    if (!firstName.trim() || !lastName.trim() || !email.trim()) {
      alert("Please enter all profile fields");
      return;
    }

    setProfile({
      firstName: firstName.trim(),
      lastName: lastName.trim(),
      email: email.trim(),
    });
    setIsEditing(false);
    alert("Profile updated successfully");
  };
  return (
    <div className="w-40 mr-75">
      <div className="card pa-50">
        <h1>User Profile</h1>
        <form>
          <div className="layout-column mb-15">
            <label htmlFor="firstname" className="mb-3">
              First Name
            </label>
            {isEditing ? (
              <input
                type="text"
                id="firstName"
                placeholder="Enter First Name"
                data-testid="firstNameInput"
                value={data.firstName}
                onChange={(e) =>
                  setData({ ...data, firstName: e.target.value })
                }
              />
            ) : (
              <div className="card pa-8" data-testid="firstNameDiv">
                {profile.firstName}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          <div className="layout-column mb-15">
            <label htmlFor="lastname" className="mb-3">
              Last Name
            </label>
            {isEditing ? (
              <input
                type="text"
                id="lastName"
                placeholder="Enter Last Name"
                data-testid="lastNameInput"
                value={data.lastName}
                onChange={(e) => setData({ ...data, lastName: e.target.value })}
              />
            ) : (
              <div className="card pa-8" data-testid="lastNameDiv">
                {profile.lastName}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          <div className="layout-column mb-30">
            <label htmlFor="email" className="mb-3">
              Email
            </label>
            {isEditing ? (
              <input
                type="text"
                id="email"
                placeholder="Enter Email"
                data-testid="emailInput"
                value={data.email}
                onChange={(e) => setData({ ...data, email: e.target.value })}
              />
            ) : (
              <div className="card pa-8" data-testid="emailDiv">
                {profile.email}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          <div className="layout-row justify-content-end">
            <button
              onClick={handleSubmit}
              type="submit"
              className="mx-0"
              data-testid="changeButton"
            >
              {!isEditing ? "Edit Profile" : "Save Changes"}
            </button>
          </div>
        </form>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default function NavBar() {
  const [active, setActive] = useState("Home");
  const TABS = ["Home", "News", "Contact", "About"];

  const getContent = () => {
    return ^\{active.toUpperCase()} PAGE^;
  };

  return (
    <div className="layout-column justify-content-center align-items-center">
      <div
        className="layout-row justify-content-around align-items-center mt-20 links"
        data-testid="navigation-tabs"
      >
        {TABS.map((tab) => (
          <a key={tab} onClick={() => setActive(tab)}>
            {tab}
          </a>
        ))}
      </div>

      <div className="card w-20 ma-0">
        <section className="card-text" data-testid="tab-content">
          <span>{getContent()}</span>
        </section>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}








25. Pagination
======================================================


pagination.js
-----------------------------------------------

const Pagination = ({ data }) => {
  const [start, setStart] = useState(0);
  const [end, setEnd] = useState(0);
  const [rows, setRows] = useState(5);
  return (
    <>
      <div className="card flex flex-col items-center gap-8 p-8 mb-8">
        {/* Heading kept from Solution styling */}
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold text-primary mb-2">
          Pagination Controls
        </h2>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
          <label className="text-sm font-medium text-primary">
            Rows per page:
          </label>
          <select
            value={rows}
            data-testid="selectInput"
            className="select w-20"
            onChange={(e) => setRows(e.target.value)}
          >
            <option value="5">5</option>
            <option value="10">10</option>
            <option value="15">15</option>
          </select>
        </div>
        <div className="button-div" data-testid="buttonDiv">
          {[...Array(Math.ceil(data.length / rows))].map((_, i) => (
            <button
              onClick={() => {
                setStart(i * rows);
                setEnd((i + 1) * rows);
              }}
              className="btn btn-secondary"
            >
              {i + 1}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Static table like in boilerplate */}
      <Table data={data.slice(start, end)} />
    </>
  );
};



Table.js
-------------------------------------------------
const Table = ({ data }) => {
  return (
    <div className="card overflow-hidden">
      <div className="overflow-x-auto">
        <table data-testid="table" className="table">
          <thead>
            <tr>
              <th>Country</th>
              <th>Capital</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody data-testid="tableBody">
            {data.map((item, index) => (
              <tr key={index}>
                <td>{item.country}</td>
                <td>{item.city}</td>
              </tr>
            ))}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};








26. Task manager
=======================================================

function Tasks() {
  const [name, setName] = useState("");
  const [priority, setPriority] = useState("");
  const [list, setList] = useState([]);

  const addTask = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (name.trim().length === 0 || priority === "" || priority <= 0) {
      toast.error("Please enter both title and task priority");
      return;
    }

    const tableData = {
      name: name.trim(),
      priority: priority,
    };

    const newList = [...list, tableData];
    const sortedList = newList.sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);
    setList(sortedList);
    setPriority("");
    setName("");
  };

  const handleDelete = (index) => {
    const filtered = [...list].filter((_, id) => id !== index);
    setList(filtered);
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col items-center w-full px-8">
      <div className="w-full max-w-5xl bg-white rounded-2xl shadow p-5 mt-12 mb-8">
        <div className="flex flex-row space-x-3 mb-6">
          <div className="bg-[#DCFAE6] text-[#18A149] rounded-lg p-4 flex items-center justify-center">
            <CirclePlus size={24} />
          </div>
          <div>
            <div className="font-bold text-md sm:text-lg">
              Create a new task
            </div>
            <div className="text-neutral-500 text-sm sm:text-base">
              Add task title and priority to create a new task
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <form className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-6 mb-3">
          <input
            data-testid="input-task-name"
            type="text"
            className="flex-1 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 px-4 py-3 text-base focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-gray-800 bg-gray-100"
            placeholder="Enter task title"
            value={name}
            onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
          />
          <input
            data-testid="input-task-priority"
            type="number"
            className="md:w-72 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 px-4 py-3 text-base focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-gray-800 bg-gray-100"
            placeholder="Enter task priority"
            value={priority}
            onChange={(e) => setPriority(e.target.value)}
          />
          <button
            onClick={addTask}
            data-testid="submit-button"
            className="h-12 px-8 rounded-md bg-black text-white font-bold text-base hover:bg-gray-900 transition"
          >
            Add
          </button>
        </form>
      </div>

      <div className="w-full max-w-5xl mb-6">
        <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold text-black">Your Tasks</h2>
      </div>
      <div className="w-full max-w-5xl bg-white rounded-2xl shadow overflow-hidden mb-8">
        <table className="w-full text-left">
          <thead>
            <tr className="border-b border-spacing-2 border-gray-200">
              <th
                className="py-4 px-6 text-base font-bold text-gray-600"
                style={{ width: "70%" }}
              >
                Task Title
              </th>
              <th
                className="py-4 px-6 text-base font-bold text-gray-600"
                style={{ width: "20%" }}
              >
                Priority
              </th>
              <th className="py-4 px-6" style={{ width: "10%" }}></th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody data-testid="tasksList">
            {list.map((item, index) => (
              <tr
                key={index}
                className="border-b border-spacing-2 border-gray-200 last:border-b-0 hover:bg-gray-50 transition"
              >
                <td className="py-2 px-6 text-neutral-500 text-base font-normal">
                  {item.name}
                </td>
                <td className="py-2 px-6 text-neutral-500 text-base font-normal">
                  {item.priority}
                </td>

                <td className="py-2 px-6">
                  <button
                    onClick={() => handleDelete(index)}
                    className="p-2 rounded"
                    aria-label="Delete task"
                  >
                    <Trash2 className="w-5 h-5 text-red-500 hover:text-red-700" />
                  </button>
                </td>
              </tr>
            ))}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}









27. Team-selection

export default function TeamSelection() {
  const [players, setPlayers] = useState(playersList);
  const [selectedPlayers, setSelectedPlayers] = useState([]);

  const sortBy = (key) => {
    const sorted = [...players].sort((a, b) => {
      if (key === "name") return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
      else if (key === "type") return a.type.localeCompare(b.type);
      else if (key === "battingSkill") return a.battingSkill - b.battingSkill;
      else if (key === "bowlingSkill") return a.bowlingSkill - b.bowlingSkill;
    });
    setPlayers(sorted);
    // Empty function - no sorting functionality
  };

  const addPlayer = (index) => {
    // Empty function - no add functionality
    const player = players?.find((_, id) => id === index);
    setSelectedPlayers([...selectedPlayers, player]);
  };

  const removePlayer = (index) => {
    // Empty function - no remove functionality
    const filtered = [...selectedPlayers].filter((_, id) => id !== index);
    setSelectedPlayers(filtered);
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col items-start gap-6 sm:gap-8 px-4 sm:px-6 md:px-8 lg:px-12 pt-8 sm:pt-12 pb-24 w-full">
      {/* Two Columns */}
      <div className="flex w-full items-start gap-6 flex-col lg:flex-row">
        {/* Available Players Section */}
        <div className="flex-1 w-full">
          <h2
            className="m-0 p-0 mb-6 font-satoshi text-2xl sm:text-[32px] leading-8 sm:leading-[44px] font-bold text-[#101828]"
            style={{ fontFeatureSettings: "'ss03' on" }}
          >
            Available Players
          </h2>
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-md border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="p-4 sm:p-6">
              <div className="overflow-hidden">
                <table
                  className="w-full table-fixed font-satoshi text-sm"
                  style={{ fontFeatureSettings: "'ss03' on" }}
                >
                  <thead>
                    <tr className="border-b border-[#ECEFF2] align-middle">
                      <th
                        data-testid="available-players-name"
                        onClick={() => sortBy("name")}
                        className="text-left py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 font-bold text-[#516778] leading-6 cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-50 w-auto sm:w-[160px]"
                      >
                        Name
                      </th>
                      <th
                        data-testid="available-players-role"
                        onClick={() => sortBy("type")}
                        className="text-left py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 font-bold text-[#516778] leading-6 cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-50"
                      >
                        Role
                      </th>
                      <th
                        data-testid="available-players-bat"
                        onClick={() => sortBy("battingSkill")}
                        className="hidden sm:table-cell text-center py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 font-bold text-[#516778] leading-6 cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-50"
                      >
                        Bat
                      </th>
                      <th
                        data-testid="available-players-bowl"
                        onClick={() => sortBy("bowlingSkill")}
                        className="hidden sm:table-cell text-center py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 font-bold text-[#516778] leading-6 cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-50"
                      >
                        Bowl
                      </th>
                    </tr>
                  </thead>
                  <tbody data-testid="available-players-table-body">
                    {players.map((player, index) => (
                      <tr
                        data-testid={^available-\{player.name
                          .split(" ")
                          .join("-")}-row^}
                        key={index}
                        className="border-b border-[#ECEFF2] hover:bg-gray-50 align-middle"
                      >
                        <td
                          data-testid={^available-\{player.name
                            .split(" ")
                            .join("-")}-name^}
                          className="flex items-center gap-3 py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 text-[#101828] leading-5 w-auto sm:w-[180px] truncate"
                        >
                          {player.name}
                        </td>
                        <td className="py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 text-[#516778] leading-5 truncate whitespace-nowrap">
                          {player.type}
                        </td>
                        <td className="hidden sm:table-cell py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 text-center text-[#516778] leading-5">
                          {player.battingSkill}
                        </td>
                        <td className="hidden sm:table-cell py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 text-center text-[#516778] leading-5">
                          {player.bowlingSkill}
                        </td>
                        <td className="py-0 px-0 text-center w-12 sm:w-[68px]">
                          <button
                            data-testid={^available-\{player.name
                              .split(" ")
                              .join("-")}-select^}
                            onClick={() => addPlayer(index)}
                            disabled={selectedPlayers.some(
                              (x) => x.name === player.name
                            )}
                            aria-label="Select player"
                            className="w-12 sm:w-[68px] px-3 sm:px-6 py-2 sm:py-3 flex items-center justify-center gap-3 border-b border-[#ECEFF2] hover:bg-gray-50"
                          >
                            <span className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-12 h-6 rounded-full bg-green-100">
                              <img src="/assets/arrow.svg" alt="Select" />
                            </span>
                          </button>
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                    ))}
                  </tbody>
                </table>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Selected Players Section */}
        <div className="flex-1 w-full">
          <h2
            className="m-0 p-0 mb-6 font-satoshi text-2xl sm:text-[32px] leading-8 sm:leading-[44px] font-bold text-[#101828]"
            style={{ fontFeatureSettings: "'ss03' on" }}
          >
            Selected Players
          </h2>
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-md border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="p-4 sm:p-6">
              <div className="overflow-hidden">
                <table
                  className="w-full table-fixed font-satoshi text-sm"
                  style={{ fontFeatureSettings: "'ss03' on" }}
                >
                  <thead>
                    <tr className="border-b border-[#ECEFF2] align-middle">
                      <th className="text-left py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 font-bold text-[#516778] leading-6 w-auto sm:w-[180px]">
                        Name
                      </th>
                      <th className="text-left py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 font-bold text-[#516778] leading-6">
                        Role
                      </th>
                      <th className="hidden sm:table-cell text-center py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 font-bold text-[#516778] leading-6">
                        Bat
                      </th>
                      <th className="hidden sm:table-cell text-center py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 font-bold text-[#516778] leading-6">
                        Bowl
                      </th>
                    </tr>
                  </thead>
                  <tbody data-testid="selected-players-table-body">
                    {/* Empty - no players selected */}
                    {selectedPlayers.map((player, index) => (
                      <tr
                        data-testid={^available-\{player.name
                          .split(" ")
                          .join("-")}-row^}
                        key={index}
                        className="border-b border-[#ECEFF2] hover:bg-gray-50 align-middle"
                      >
                        <td
                          data-testid={^available-\{player.name
                            .split(" ")
                            .join("-")}-name^}
                          className="flex items-center gap-3 py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 text-[#101828] leading-5 w-auto sm:w-[180px] truncate"
                        >
                          {player.name}
                        </td>
                        <td className="py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 text-[#516778] leading-5 truncate whitespace-nowrap">
                          {player.type}
                        </td>
                        <td className="hidden sm:table-cell py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 text-center text-[#516778] leading-5">
                          {player.battingSkill}
                        </td>
                        <td className="hidden sm:table-cell py-2 sm:py-3 px-3 sm:px-6 text-center text-[#516778] leading-5">
                          {player.bowlingSkill}
                        </td>
                        <td className="py-0 px-0 text-center w-12 sm:w-[68px]">
                          <button
                            data-testid={^selected-\{player.name
                              .split(" ")
                              .join("-")}-remove^}
                            onClick={() => removePlayer(index)}
                            aria-label="Select player"
                            className="w-12 sm:w-[68px] px-3 sm:px-6 py-2 sm:py-3 flex items-center justify-center gap-3 border-b border-[#ECEFF2] hover:bg-gray-50"
                          >
                            Delete
                          </button>
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                    ))}
                  </tbody>
                </table>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

Teamlist.js

const TeamList = () => {
  const teamList = [
    {
      name: "Team1",
      channels: [
        { name: "Channel1", id: 1 },
        { name: "Channel2", id: 2 },
      ],
    },
    {
      name: "Team2",
      channels: [
        { name: "Channel1", id: 1 },
        { name: "Channel2", id: 2 },
      ],
    },
  ];

  const [list, setList] = useState(teamList);
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");

  const addTeam = () => {
    const newTeam = { name: input, channels: [] };
    setList([...list, newTeam]);
    setInput("");
  };

  return (
    <div className="w-50 mx-auto">
      <div className="card w-35 mt-50 mx-auto px-10 py-15">
        <div className="layout-column" data-testid="team-list">
          {list &&
            list.map((team, id) => <Team key={id} id={id} team={team} />)}
        </div>
        <div className="layout-row">
          <input
            placeholder="Enter Team Name"
            className="team-list-input w-75"
            data-testid="team-name-input"
            value={input}
            onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
          />
          <button
            className="team-list-btn x-small w-35 h-30 pa-6 ma-0 ml-6"
            data-testid="add-team-btn"
            onClick={addTeam}
            disabled={!input || list.some((x) => x.name === input)}
          >
            Add Team
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};



Team.js
-------------------------------------------------------
const Team = ({ team, id }) => {
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const [channels, setChannels] = useState(team.channels);

  const addChannel = () => {
    let idCh = channels.length + 1;
    const newChannel = { name: input, id: idCh };
    setChannels([...channels, newChannel]);
    setInput("");
  };
  const handleDelete = (index) => {
    const filtered = [...channels].filter((x) => x.id !== index);
    setChannels(filtered);
  };
  return (
    <div>
      {team && <h4 className="mt-0 mb-6">{team.name}</h4>}
      {team && (
        <div className="layout-row justify-content-end mb-6">
          <input
            placeholder="Enter Channel Name"
            className="channel-name-input w-45 px-13"
            data-testid={"channel-name-input-" + id}
            value={input}
            onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
          />
          <button
            className="channel-name-btn x-small w-35 h-30 pa-6 ma-0 ml-6"
            data-testid={"add-channel-btn-" + id}
            onClick={addChannel}
            disabled={!input || channels.some((x) => x.name === input)}
          >
            Add Channel
          </button>
        </div>
      )}
      {team && (
        <ul className="styled mb-20 pl-25" data-testid={"channel-list-" + id}>
          {channels &&
            channels.map((channel) => (
              <li
                key={channel.id}
                className="flex slide-up-fade-in justify-content-between align-items-center pl-10 pr-5 py-6 mt-0 mb-6"
              >
                <span>{channel.name}</span>
                <button
                  data-testid={"remove-channel-button-" + id + channel.id}
                  className="icon-only x-small danger ma-0 pa-0"
                  onClick={() => handleDelete(channel.id)}
                >
                  <i className="material-icons">delete</i>
                </button>
              </li>
            ))}
        </ul>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

Addperson.js

export default function AddPerson({ onButtonClick }) {
	const addPerson = (event) => {
		event.preventDefault();
		if (name !== "" && number !== 0 && String(number).length === 10 && email !== "") {
			onButtonClick("", person);
		}
		else {
			event.preventDefault()
		}
	};
	let [person, setPerson] = useState({
		name: "",
		number: 0,
		email: "",
	});
	let { name, number, email } = person;
	const handleChange = (event) => {
		setPerson({ ...person, [event.target.name]: event.target.value });
	};
	return (
		<section>
			<div className="card pa-30 mr-30">
				<form data-testid="add-person-form" onSubmit={addPerson}>
					<div className="layout-column mb-15">
						<label htmlFor="name" className="mb-3">
							Person Name
						</label>
						<input
							type="text"
							placeholder="Enter Person Name"
							name="name"
							value={name}
							onChange={handleChange}
							data-testid="person-name-input"
						/>
					</div>
					<div className="layout-column mb-15">
						<label htmlFor="number" className="mb-3">
							Phone Number
						</label>
						<input
							type="number"
							placeholder="Enter Phone Number"
							name="number"
							value={number}
							onChange={handleChange}
							data-testid="phone-number-input"
						/>
					</div>
					<div className="layout-column mb-30">
						<label htmlFor="email" className="mb-3">
							Email
						</label>
						<input
							type="email"
							placeholder="Enter Email Address"
							name="email"
							value={email}
							onChange={handleChange}
							data-testid="person-email-input"
						/>
					</div>
					<div className="layout-row justify-content-end">
						<button type="submit" className="mx-0" data-testid="add-person-button">
							Add Person
						</button>
					</div>
				</form>
			</div>
		</section>
	);
}






30. Timer component
========================================================

export default function Timer({ initial }) {
  const [timer, setTimer] = useState(initial);
  const [flag, setFlag] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    let id;
    if (flag && timer > 0) {
      id = setInterval(() => {
        setTimer((prev) => (prev > 0 ? prev - 1 : 0));
      }, 1000);
    }
    return () => clearInterval(id);
  }, [timer, flag]);

  const stopping = () => {
    setFlag(false);
  };
  return (
    <div className="timer-container">
      {/* Timer Card */}
      <div className="timer-card">
        {/* Timer Display */}
        <div className="timer-display-wrapper">
          <div className="timer-label">Timer</div>

          {/* Static placeholder (no logic) */}
          <div className="timer-value" data-testid="timer-value">
            {/* leave empty like original boilerplate, or show {initial} if desired */}
            {timer}
          </div>

          <div className="timer-subtitle">seconds remaining</div>
        </div>
        {/* Stop Button (no handler) */}
        <button
          onClick={stopping}
          className="btn-stop"
          data-testid="stop-button"
        >
          <svg
            className="btn-icon"
            fill="none"
            stroke="currentColor"
            viewBox="0 0 24 24"
          >
            <rect
              x="6"
              y="6"
              width="12"
              height="12"
              strokeWidth="2"
              strokeLinecap="round"
              strokeLinejoin="round"
            />
          </svg>
          Stop Timer
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

Pokemon details.js

export const PokemonDetails = () => {
  const [pokemon, setPokemon] = React.useState(null);
  const [id, setId] = React.useState(0);
  const getPokemonById = async (id) => {
    if (id >= 1 && id <= 151) {
      const data = await fetch(
        ^https://jsonmock.hackerrank.com/api/pokemon?id=\{id}^
      );
      const json = await data.json();
      const dataArr = json.data;
      setPokemon(dataArr);
    } else {
      alert("Pokemon ID must be between 1 and 151");
      return;
    }
  };

  const settingnext = (id) => {
    getPokemonById(id);
  };
  const settingprev = (id) => {
    getPokemonById(id);
  };

  return (
    <div className="mt-50 layout-column justify-content-center align-items-center">
      {pokemon && (
        <>
          <Pokemon pokemon={pokemon} />
          <p>
            <button
              disabled={!pokemon?.prev_evolution}
              onClick={() =>
                settingprev(
                  pokemon.prev_evolution[pokemon.prev_evolution.length - 1].num
                )
              }
              data-testid="pokemon-prev"
            >
              Previous Evolution
            </button>
            <button
              disabled={!pokemon?.next_evolution}
              onClick={() => settingnext(pokemon.next_evolution[0].num)}
              data-testid="pokemon-next"
            >
              Next Evolution
            </button>
          </p>
        </>
      )}
      <p>
        <input
          data-testid="id-input"
          value={id}
          onChange={(e) => setId(e.target.value)}
          type="number"
          placeholder="Pokemon Id"
        ></input>
        <button
          data-testid="random-pokemon"
          onClick={() => getPokemonById(id)}
          className="text"
        >
          Get Pokemon
        </button>
      </p>
    </div>
  );
};
